Question 1: Get List of ACC Teams¶

Read the acc_teams.json file into a pandas DataFrame object and save the list of ACC teams into a list of tuples (team_id, team_name) named acc_teams. (3 points)

In [3]:
Student's answer(Top)
acc_teams = []
# YOUR CODE HERE
# raise NotImplementedError()

def read_acc_team(file_name = "acc_teams.json"):
    import json
    fp= open(file_name,"r")
    team_list = json.load(fp)
    fp.close()
    team_list_df = pd.DataFrame(team_list)
    return team_list_df
acc_teams_df = read_acc_team()
acc_teams = [(int(i), acc_teams_df['name'].loc[i]) for i in acc_teams_df.index.values.tolist() ]
acc_teams

import requests

    roster = extract_team_roster(team_id, team_name)
    roster_info = {'team_id': team_id, 'team_name': team_name, 'roster':roster}
    
    team_rosters.append(roster_info)

Question 3. Save the Rosters to a JSON File.¶

Write code segment to save the rosters of all ACC team to a JSON File named 'acc_team_rosters.json`. (2 points)

In [8]:
Student's answer(Top)
# YOUR CODE HERE
# raise NotImplementedError()
def save_rosters(rosters, file_name = 'acc_team_rosters.json'):
    fp = open(file_name,'w+')
    rosters_json = json.dumps(rosters)
    fp.write(rosters_json)
    fp.close()
    
save_rosters(team_rosters)
